384.95, # K (from PLAN: Tc = 384.95 K)\n \'critical_pressure\': 4.136, # MPa (from PLAN: Pc = 4.136 MPa)\n \'critical_density\': 558, # kg/m¬≥ (from PLAN)\n \'acentric_factor\': 0.176, # (from PLAN)\n \'gas_constant\': 8.314 # J/(mol¬∑K)\n}\n\nprint(f"\\nFreon-12 Properties:")\nfor key, value in freon_properties.items():\n print(f" ‚Ä¢ {key.replace(\'_\', \' \').title()}: {value}")\n\n# Define Marianas Trench conditions (from PLAN)\nmarianas_conditions = {\n \'pressure_atm\': 1086, # atm (from PLAN: 1,086 atm)\n \'pressure_MPa\': 110.0, # MPa (from PLAN: 110.0 MPa)\n \'temperature_C\': 4, # ¬∞C (from PLAN: 4¬∞C)\n \'temperature_K\': 4 + 273.15 # K (277.15 K from PLAN)\n}\n\nprint(f"\\nMarianas Trench Conditions:")\nfor key, value in marianas_conditions.items():\n print(f" ‚Ä¢ {key.replace(\'_\', \' \').title()}: {value}")\n\n# Define calculation parameters\ncalculation_params = {\n \'freon_mass_kg\': 0.312, # kg (from PLAN)\n \'freon_mass_g\': 0.312 * 1000, # g\n \'moles\': (0.312 * 1000) / freon_properties[\'molecular_weight\'] # mol\n}\n\nprint(f"\\nCalculation Parameters:")\nprint(f" ‚Ä¢ Freon-12 Mass: {calculation_params[\'freon_mass_kg\']} kg ({calculation_params[\'freon_mass_g\']} g)")\nprint(f" ‚Ä¢ Number of Moles: {calculation_params[\'moles\']:.6f} mol")\n\nprint(f"\\n=== STEP 2: IMPLEMENTING PENG-ROBINSON EQUATION OF STATE ===")\n\n# Peng-Robinson equation of state implementation\ndef peng_robinson_eos(T, P, Tc, Pc, omega, R=8.314):\n """\n Calculate molar volume using Peng-Robinson equation of state\n \n Parameters:\n T: Temperature (K)\n P: Pressure (Pa)\n Tc: Critical temperature (K)\n Pc: Critical pressure (Pa)\n omega: Acentric factor\n R: Gas constant (J/(mol¬∑K))\n \n Returns:\n Molar volume (m¬≥/mol)\n """\n \n print(f"\\n--- Peng-Robinson EOS Calculation ---")\n print(f"Input conditions:")\n print(f" T = {T} K")\n print(f" P = {P/1e6:.3f} MPa ({P/101325:.1f} atm)")\n print(f" Tc = {Tc} K")\n print(f" Pc = {Pc/1e6:.3f} MPa")\n print(f" œâ = {omega}")\n \n # Calculate reduced temperature and pressure\n Tr = T / Tc\n Pr = P / Pc\n \n print(f"\\nReduced properties:")\n print(f" Tr = T/Tc = {Tr:.4f}")\n print(f" Pr = P/Pc = {Pr:.4f}")\n \n # Peng-Robinson parameters\n a_alpha = 0.45724 * (R**2 * Tc**2) / Pc\n b = 0.07780 * R * Tc / Pc\n \n # Temperature-dependent alpha function\n kappa = 0.37464 + 1.54226 * omega - 0.26992 * omega**2\n alpha = (1 + kappa * (1 - math.sqrt(Tr)))**2\n a = a_alpha * alpha\n \n print(f"\\nPeng-Robinson parameters:")\n print(f" a‚ÇÄ = {a_alpha:.6e} Pa¬∑m‚Å∂/mol¬≤")\n print(f" b = {b:.6e} m¬≥/mol")\n print(f" Œ∫ = {kappa:.6f}")\n print(f" Œ± = {alpha:.6f}")\n print(f" a = {a:.6e} Pa¬∑m‚Å∂/mol¬≤")\n \n # Solve cubic equation for compressibility factor Z\n # Z¬≥ - (1-B)Z¬≤ + (A-2B-3B¬≤)Z - (AB-B¬≤-B¬≥) = 0\n \n A = a * P / (R**2 * T**2)\n B = b * P / (R * T)\n \n print(f"\\nDimensionless parameters:")\n print(f" A = aP/(RT)¬≤ = {A:.6f}")\n print(f" B = bP/(RT) = {B:.6f}")\n \n # Cubic equation coefficients\n c0 = -(A*B - B**2 - B**3)\n c1 = A - 2*B - 3*B**2\n c2 = -(1 - B)\n c3 = 1\n \n print(f"\\nCubic equation: Z¬≥ + ({c2:.6f})Z¬≤ + ({c1:.6f})Z + ({c0:.6f}) = 0")\n \n # Solve cubic equation using Cardano\'s method\n def solve_cubic(a, b, c, d):\n """Solve cubic equation ax¬≥ + bx¬≤ + cx + d = 0"""\n # Convert to depressed cubic t¬≥ + pt + q = 0\n p = (3*a*c - b**2) / (3*a**2)\n q = (2*b**3 - 9*a*b*c + 27*a**2*d) / (27*a**3)\n \n # Discriminant\n discriminant = (q/2)**2 + (p/3)**3\n \n if discriminant > 0:\n # One real root\n u = (-q/2 + math.sqrt(discriminant))**(1/3) if (-q/2 + math.sqrt(discriminant)) >= 0 else -(abs(-q/2 + math.sqrt(discriminant))**(1/3))\n v = (-q/2 - math.sqrt(discriminant))**(1/3) if (-q/2 - math.sqrt(discriminant)) >= 0 else -(abs(-q/2 - math.sqrt(discriminant))**(1/3))\n t = u + v\n z = t - b/(3*a)\n return [z]\n else:\n # Three real roots\n import cmath\n m = 2 * math.sqrt(-p/3)\n theta = (1/3) * cmath.acos(3*q/(p*m)).real\n \n z1 = m * math.cos(theta) - b/(3*a)\n z2 = m * math.cos(theta + 2*math.pi/3) - b/(3*a)\n z3 = m * math.cos(theta + 4*math.pi/3) - b/(3*a)\n \n return sorted([z1, z2, z3])\n \n # Solve for compressibility factor Z\n z_roots = solve_cubic(c3, c2, c1, c0)\n \n print(f"\\nCompressibility factor roots:")\n for i, z in enumerate(z_roots):\n print(f" Z{i+1} = {z:.6f}")\n \n # Select appropriate root (liquid phase - smallest positive root)\n # At high pressure like Marianas Trench, Freon-12 will be in liquid phase\n valid_roots = [z for z in z_roots if z > 0]\n if valid_roots:\n Z = min(valid_roots) # Liquid phase (smallest positive root)\n print(f"\\nSelected compressibility factor (liquid phase): Z = {Z:.6f}")\n else:\n print("\\nError: No valid positive roots found")\n return None\n \n # Calculate molar volume\n V_molar = Z * R * T / P # m¬≥/mol\n \n print(f"\\nMolar volume calculation:")\n print(f" V = ZRT/P = ({Z:.6f})({R})({T})/{P:.0f}")\n print(f" V = {V_molar:.6e} m¬≥/mol")\n \n return V_molar, Z\n\nprint(f"\\n=== STEP 3: PERFORMING VOLUME CALCULATION ===")\n\n# Convert pressure to Pa for calculations\nP_Pa = marianas_conditions[\'pressure_MPa\'] * 1e6 # Convert MPa to Pa\nPc_Pa = freon_properties[\'critical_pressure\'] * 1e6 # Convert MPa to Pa\n\nprint(f"\\nPressure conversion:")\nprint(f" Operating pressure: {marianas_conditions[\'pressure_MPa\']} MPa = {P_Pa:.0f} Pa")\nprint(f" Critical pressure: {freon_properties[\'critical_pressure\']} MPa = {Pc_Pa:.0f} Pa")\n\n# Calculate molar volume using Peng-Robinson EOS\nresult = peng_robinson_eos(\n T=marianas_conditions[\'temperature_K\'],\n P=P_Pa,\n Tc=freon_properties[\'critical_temperature\'],\n Pc=Pc_Pa,\n omega=freon_properties[\'acentric_factor\']\n)\n\nif result:\n V_molar, Z = result\n \n # Calculate total volume for 0.312 kg of Freon-12\n total_volume_m3 = V_molar *
